⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
قيل : تركيب الأنواع الثلاثة من امتزاج العناصر الأربعة، إلا أن الغالب على الشياطين عنصر النار ، وعلى الآخرين عنصر الهواء. وذلك أن امتزاج العناصر قد لا يكون على القرب من الاعتدال، بل على قدر صالح من غلبة أحدها . فإن كانت الغلبة للأرضية، يكون الممتزج مائلاً إلى عنصر الأرض، وإن كانت للمائية، فإلى الماء، أو للهوائية فإلى الهواء، أو للنارية فإلى النار، لا يبرح ولا يفارق إلا بالأحياز، أو بأن يكون حيواناً فيفارق بالاختيار، وليس لهذه الغلبة حد معين، بل تختلف إلى مراتب، بحسب أنواع الممتزجات التي تسكن هذا العنصر، ولكون الهواء والنار في غاية اللطافة والشفيف كانت الملائكة والجن والشياطين، بحيث يدخلون المنافذ والمضايق حتى أجواف الإنسان، ولا يرون بحس البصر، إلا إذا اكتسوا من الممتزجات الآخر التي يغلب عليها الأرضية والمائية جلابيب وغواشي فيرون في أبدان كأبدان الناس أو غيره من الحيوانات، والملائكة كثيراً ما تعاون الإنسان على أعمال يعجز هو عنها بقوته كالغلبة على الأعداء، والطيران في الهواء، والمشي على الماء، وتحفظه خصوصاً المضطر عن كثير من الآفات، وأما الجن والشياطين فيخالطون بعض الأناسي، ويعاونونهم على السحر والطلسمات والنيرنجات وما يشكل ذلك. قال ولا يمتنع أن يكتسبوا أحياناً جلابيب من أجسام كثيفة، فيراهم الإنسان، أو يكون فيهم من العنصر الكثيف ما يقتضي الظهور لبعض الأبصار، وفي بعض الأحوال، وأن يكون في أمزجتهم وصورهم النوعية، ما يقتضي حفظ التركيب عند الانحلال والتشكل بالأشكال وأما على القول بالقادر المختار فلا إشكال
It is said: The composition of the three types is from the mixture of the four elements, except that the dominant element for devils is fire, and for the others is air. That is because the mixture of elements may not be close to equilibrium, but rather to a suitable degree of predominance of one of them. If the predominance is earthy, the mixture inclines to the element of earth; if watery, to water; if airy, to air; if fiery, to fire; it does not leave nor separate except by constraint, or by being an animal it separates by choice. There is no fixed limit for this predominance, but it varies in degrees according to the types of mixtures that inhabit this element. Because air and fire are extremely subtle and transparent, the angels, jinn, and devils are such that they enter narrow passages and tight spaces, even the cavities of humans, and are not seen by the sense of sight unless they acquire from the other mixtures dominated by earth and water garments and covers, and then they are seen in bodies like the bodies of humans or other animals. The angels often assist humans in deeds that humans are incapable of by their own strength, such as overcoming enemies, flying in the air, walking on water, and protecting the distressed person from many afflictions. As for jinn and devils, they mingle with some humans and assist them in sorcery, talismans, incantations, and the like. He said: And it is not impossible that they sometimes acquire garments from dense bodies, so that humans see them, or that among them there is from the dense element what necessitates appearance to some visions in some states, and that in their mixtures and specific forms there is what necessitates preservation of composition during dissolution and forming into shapes. And as for the view of the omnipotent chooser (al-Qādir al-Mukhtār), there is no problem.
Source pages p. 369

Commentary
This passage explains the natural composition of angels, jinn, and devils according to the theory of elemental mixture. It begins by stating that these three types are composed from the four elements (earth, water, air, fire), but with a predominance: devils are dominated by fire, while angels and jinn are dominated by air. The mixture is not necessarily balanced; rather, one element can predominate to a suitable degree. The author then describes how the predominance of each element inclines the mixture towards that element. The mixture does not separate from its elemental source except by force (al-ahyāz) or by being an animal that can move by choice. There is no fixed limit to this predominance; it varies according to the types of mixtures that inhabit each element. Because air and fire are extremely subtle and transparent (al-latāfa wa al-shafīf), these beings can enter narrow passages and even the cavities of humans, and are invisible to the human eye. However, they can become visible by acquiring garments or covers (jalābīb wa ghawāshī) from denser elements (earth and water), appearing in bodies resembling humans or animals. The passage then notes that angels often aid humans in superhuman acts, while jinn and devils interact with humans in sorcery and related arts. Finally, the author adds that it is not impossible for them to occasionally acquire dense bodies for visibility, and that their specific mixtures and forms allow them to dissolve and reform shapes. He concludes that on the view of an omnipotent chooser (God), there is no difficulty. The commentary follows the source's order, explaining each point as presented.

Key Terms
امتزاج العناصر
الغلبة
اللطافة
الشفيف

Key Terms from Source Passage

Misconception & Correction
Misconception: That angels, jinn, and devils are purely spiritual beings with no physical composition.
Correction: The passage asserts they are composed from the four material elements, albeit with a predominance of air or fire, giving them subtle bodies.

Checkpoint
According to the passage, what is the dominant element for angels and jinn?
A) Earth
B) Water
C) Air
D) Fire

Key Takeaway
Angels, jinn, and devils have physical compositions from the four elements, with devils dominated by fire and the others by air, but the mixture varies without a fixed limit.

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
If your own spiritual 'mixture' is not fixed, what does the predominance of certain traits (e.g., anger, pride, humility) reveal about your current state? Are you tending toward the fire of selfish desires or the air of spiritual lightness? What concrete step can you take today to adjust your predominance toward what Allah loves?
?
The passage notes that devils are dominated by fire, a source of destruction. Reflect on a time when 'fire' – like uncontrolled anger or envy – consumed you and led to sin. How can you extinguish that fire using the means Allah has provided, such as repentance and seeking refuge?
?
Consider that angels and jinn have physical compositions that determine their actions. You too have a physical body that influences your spirituality. Are you feeding your body in a way that supports obedience or hinders it? What one change in your physical routine could help you draw closer to Allah?

Causality and Created Things
intermediate
10 min
The Visibility and Human Interaction of Angels, Jinn, and Devils
Explains invisibility, visibility conditions, and types of human interaction.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will understand why angels, jinn, and devils are usually invisible, how they can become visible, and the nature of their interactions with humans.

Core Idea
Subtle elemental composition allows invisibility, but they can manifest through dense bodies.

This passage explains how the subtlety of air and fire enables angels, jinn, and devils to enter narrow spaces and remain unseen. It then describes how they can become visible by acquiring denser coverings and outlines their typical interactions with humans, from angelic assistance to demonic sorcery.

Guided Path
1
Read the passage on visibility and interaction
Read the Arabic passage and its translation to grasp the reasons for invisibility and the conditions for visibility.
Focus on the terms 'اللطافة' (subtlety) and 'الشفيف' (transparency).
2
Understand the mechanism of invisibility
Because air and fire are extremely subtle, these beings can enter even the cavities of humans and are not seen. They must acquire garments (جلابيب وغواشي) from earth/water elements to become visible.
Visibility is an exception, not the norm.
3
Learn about their interactions with humans
Angels assist humans in superhuman acts like overcoming enemies or walking on water. Jinn and devils assist in sorcery and talismans. The passage also notes the possibility of them taking on dense bodies temporarily.
This shows a range of interactions from benevolent to harmful.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Misconception & Correction
Misconception: That angels, jinn, and devils can be seen by humans at any time or are always visible.
Correction: The passage states they are usually invisible and only become visible when they take on dense coverings.

Checkpoint
According to the passage, what must angels, jinn, and devils acquire to become visible?
A) A body made entirely of fire
B) Garments from mixtures dominated by earth and water
C) Permission from God
D) A special incantation

Key Takeaway
Angels, jinn, and devils are usually invisible due to their subtle composition, but can become visible through dense coverings, and they interact with humans in distinct ways.

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
When you consider that angels and jinn are constantly around you, unseen, but can take on physical forms to interact with humans, how does this change your awareness of your actions and intentions? Are you living as if every corner of your life is witnessed by these beings?
?
The passage says angels assist humans in superhuman tasks like overcoming enemies and protecting the distressed. Have you ever felt such assistance? If not, could it be that your lack of reliance on Allah and His angels prevents you from experiencing their help? What will you do today to actively seek angelic assistance through piety and trust?
?
The mention of jinn aiding in sorcery reminds us that supernatural help can come from evil sources. Are there any areas in your life where you are seeking shortcuts or power through questionable means, rather than relying solely on Allah? Reflect on a specific habit or desire you need to purify.
